| mid_score | post_score | .89 | [.86, .92] | < .001 | 206 |
| mid_score | outcome_reg | .30 | [.17, .43] | < .001 | 191 |
| post_score | outcome_reg | .27 | [.13, .40] | < .001 | 191 |


*Note.* Two-tailed tests. Missing values handled pairwise. Partial correlations control for age,income. 95% CI computed via Fisher's z.

*Note.* Missing values handled complete. Test-retest method: pearson. 95% CI computed via Fisher's z.

## Narrative

Overall: Test-retest pearson = 0.74, 95% CI [0.67, 0.79], p < .001, n = 234. Missing = 6 (2.5%).

---

---

- Grouping variable: None
- Method: spearman

# Mixed Models: Tests of Fixed Effects

## Analysis

- Formula: post_score ~ group2 + gender + (1|site)
- Random effects: (1|site)

- DF method: satterthwaite
- Sum of squares type: III
- Confidence level: 0.95
- Optimizer: bobyqa
- Optimizer maxfun: 100000
- Diagnostics: Yes
- Rounding digits: 2

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| group2 | 1.00 | 222.00 | 33.10 | < .001 |
| gender | 2.00 | 222.00 | 2.53 | = .082 |


*Note.* Type III tests of fixed effects. df method: satterthwaite.

group2treatment: b = 7.04, SE = 1.22, t(222.00) = 5.75, p < .001, CI [4.63, 9.46].

genderM: b = -.96, SE = 1.25, t(222.00) = -.77, p = .441, CI [-3.43, 1.50].

genderO: b = 5.71, SE = 3.03, t(222.00) = 1.88, p = .061, CI [-.26, 11.68].

# Mediation (SEM)

## Analysis

- Analysis: mediation
- X variables: x1
- Mediators: mediator
- Y variables: outcome_reg
- Covariates: x2, x3
- Estimator: MLR
- Missing handling: fiml
- Standard errors: robust
- Confidence interval: standard
- Confidence level: 0.95
- Standardization: std.all
- Fit indices: chisq, df, cfi, tli, rmsea, srmr, pvalue
- Bootstrap: No
- Rounding digits: 2

**Table 2**

*Mediation Parameter Estimates*

| Path | Label | b | SE | z | p | CI low | CI high | Std |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| mediator ~ x1 | a1 | .55 | .07 | 7.77 | < .001 | .41 | .68 | .40 |
| mediator ~ x2 |  | .40 | .06 | 6.64 | < .001 | .28 | .52 | .36 |
| mediator ~ x3 |  | -.08 | .13 | -.63 | = .527 | -.34 | .17 | -.03 |
| outcome_reg ~ x1 | c_prime | .18 | .08 | 2.32 | = .020 | .03 | .33 | .12 |
| outcome_reg ~ mediator | b1 | .59 | .07 | 8.31 | < .001 | .45 | .73 | .52 |
| outcome_reg ~ x2 |  | .22 | .08 | 2.94 | = .003 | .07 | .37 | .17 |
| outcome_reg ~ x3 |  | .07 | .14 | .47 | = .637 | -.21 | .35 | .02 |
| x1 ~~ x2 |  | .44 | .00 |  |  | .44 | .44 | .39 |
| x1 ~~ x3 |  | .07 | .00 |  |  | .07 | .07 | .14 |
| x2 ~~ x3 |  | .02 | .00 |  |  | .02 | .02 | .03 |
| indirect_mediator := a1*b1 | indirect_mediator | .32 | .06 | 5.30 | < .001 | .20 | .44 | .21 |
| total_indirect := indirect_mediator | total_indirect | .32 | .06 | 5.30 | < .001 | .20 | .44 | .21 |
| total := c_prime+total_indirect | total | .50 | .09 | 5.93 | < .001 | .34 | .67 | .33 |


*Note.* Estimator = MLR. Missing = FIML. SE = robust. CI = standard, 95%. Standardization = std.all. N = 240.

## Narrative

Model fit: chi²() = .00, CFI = 1.00, TLI = 1.00, RMSEA = .00, SRMR = .00.

R²: mediator = .40; outcome_reg = .48.

indirect_mediator: b = .32, SE = .06, p < .001, 95% CI [.20, .44].

total_indirect: b = .32, SE = .06, p < .001, 95% CI [.20, .44].

total: b = .50, SE = .09, p < .001, 95% CI [.34, .67].

# Mediation (SEM)

## Analysis

- Analysis: mediation
- X variables: x1
- Mediators: mediator
- Y variables: outcome_reg
- Covariates: x2, x3
- Estimator: MLR
- Missing handling: fiml
- Standard errors: robust
- Confidence interval: standard
- Confidence level: 0.95
- Standardization: std.all
- Fit indices: chisq, df, cfi, tli, rmsea, srmr, pvalue
- Bootstrap: No
- Rounding digits: 2

*Mediation Parameter Estimates*

| Path | Label | b | SE | z | p | CI low | CI high | Std |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| mediator ~ x1 | a1 | .55 | .07 | 7.77 | < .001 | .41 | .68 | .40 |
| mediator ~ x2 |  | .40 | .06 | 6.64 | < .001 | .28 | .52 | .36 |
| mediator ~ x3 |  | -.08 | .13 | -.63 | = .527 | -.34 | .17 | -.03 |
| outcome_reg ~ x1 | c_prime | .18 | .08 | 2.32 | = .020 | .03 | .33 | .12 |
| outcome_reg ~ mediator | b1 | .59 | .07 | 8.31 | < .001 | .45 | .73 | .52 |
| outcome_reg ~ x2 |  | .22 | .08 | 2.94 | = .003 | .07 | .37 | .17 |
| outcome_reg ~ x3 |  | .07 | .14 | .47 | = .637 | -.21 | .35 | .02 |
| x1 ~~ x2 |  | .44 | .00 |  |  | .44 | .44 | .39 |
| x1 ~~ x3 |  | .07 | .00 |  |  | .07 | .07 | .14 |
| x2 ~~ x3 |  | .02 | .00 |  |  | .02 | .02 | .03 |
| indirect_mediator := a1*b1 | indirect_mediator | .32 | .06 | 5.30 | < .001 | .20 | .44 | .21 |
| total_indirect := indirect_mediator | total_indirect | .32 | .06 | 5.30 | < .001 | .20 | .44 | .21 |
| total := c_prime+total_indirect | total | .50 | .09 | 5.93 | < .001 | .34 | .67 | .33 |


*Note.* Estimator = MLR. Missing = FIML. SE = robust. CI = standard, 95%. Standardization = std.all. N = 240.

# Nonparametric Tests

## Analysis

- Test selection: friedman
- Mode: friedman
- Within-subjects variables: pre_score, mid_score, post_score
- Subject ID: id
- Post-hoc method: none
